# Matter-Certified Devices

> Agent-friendly reference of every device certified for **Matter**, the smart-home
> interoperability standard. Use this to know which product categories and which
> specific products are officially Matter-compatible when building on top of Matter.

**Source:** [CSA Distributed Compliance Ledger (DCL)](https://on.dcl.csa-iot.org) — the canonical public registry maintained by the Connectivity Standards Alliance. Every certified Matter product is written here; this file is generated directly from it.

**Generated:** 2026-06-20  
**Devices:** 4,645 certified models  
**Vendors:** 404  
**Device categories:** 49

Each row is one certified product. `VID`/`PID` are the Matter Vendor ID and Product ID (hex), the unique identifiers the protocol uses on the wire and in the DCL. Regenerate anytime with `npm run matter`.
